alhadu al'adnaa limustawaa allawn al'ahmaru. alhadu al'adnaa lilqimat almaqbulat hu 0 walhadu al'aqsaa lilqimat almaqbulat hu 255.
'adnaa mustawan lilawn al'akhdari. alhadu al'adnaa lilqimat almaqbulat hu 0 walhadu al'aqsaa lilqimat almaqbulat hu 255.
alhadu al'adnaa limustawaa allawn al'azraqa. alhadu al'adnaa lilqimat almaqbulat hu 0 walhadu al'aqsaa lilqimat almaqbulat hu 255.
alhadu al'adnaa limustawaa alluwn. 'adnaa qimat maqbulat hi 0 wa'aqsaa qimat maqbulat hi 255 li 255 lwnan 'aw 16 li 16 lwnan.
alhadu al'aqsaa limustawaa allawn al'ahmaru. alhadu al'adnaa lilqimat almaqbulat hu 0 walhadu al'aqsaa lilqimat almaqbulat hu 255.

hadath khataan fi altaebir aleadii 'athna' muealajat alnas. tahaqaq min bina' jumlat altaebir aleadi wahawal maratan 'ukhraa. 'iidha hadath aintiha' almuhlati, fata'akad min eadam takrar al'amr kthyran (la takun jshean).
wajahat 'adawat alsafhat alrayiysiat khtaan eind muhawalat muealajat talabka. yurjaa alta'akud min 'iidkhal jamie albayanat allaazimat bishakl sahihin.
lisu' alhaz, fa'iina alfashal al'akhir ghayr maerufun, lidha la naerif bialdabt ma alkhata aladhi hadatha. wamae dhalika, qad yakun min almufid aistisharat sijilaat tashih 'akhta' alnawaati.

takhir muahad
'iidha kan shyhan, fa'iinah ymkkn takhir alkitabat almuahad lijamie shashat altawaqufu. wa'iila, fa'iinah yustakhdam qiam takhir muhadadat lishashat altawaquf.
yutih lak hadha alqism takwin kayfiat eamal tatbiq almuaqata.
yutih lak hadha alqism takwin kayfiat eamal tatbiq muaqat bumuduru.
tamkin Figlet limuaqat bumuduru
'iidha tama tamkinuhu, fasawf yustakhdam figlet limuaqat bumuduru. yurjaa mulahazat 'anah yahtaj 'iilaa shashat wahdat tahakum kabirat min 'ajl eard alwaqt bishakl sahih mae tamkin Figlet.
